DETECTOR   The PISA apparatus consists of nine independent        D051400100020 
           detection arms comprising various kinds of detectors.  D051400100021 
           Two of these arms (placed at 15. and 120. angles in    D051400100022 
           respect to the beam direction) are equipped with the   D051400100023 
           Bragg curve detectors (BCD), which permit the          D051400100024 
           Z-identification of the reaction products and          D051400100025 
           determination of their kinetic energies with low       D051400100026 
           detection energy threshold (of about 1MeV/nucleon).    D051400100027 
           The active volume of BCD's has thickness of 22 cm of   D051400100028 
           isobutane at a pressure of 206 mbar.                   D051400100029 
           (TELES,SIBAR,CSICR) The telescopes consisted of  D     D051400100030 
           silicon detectors of the following thicknesses: 50 +   D051400100031 
           400 + 6000 mu-m (at 35. and 50.), 50 + 400 mu-m (at    D051400100032 
           80.), and 50 + 400 + 1000 + 2000 mu-m (at 100 degr.).  D051400100033 
           silicon telescope at 100 deg was also supplied with    D051400100034 
           7.5 cm CsI scintillator detector standing outside the  D051400100035 
           scattering chamber.                                    D051400100036 
           At three angles (15.6., 20., and  65.), the telescopes D051400100037 
           built of silicon detectors of  the thickness of        D051400100038 
           90 + 1000 + 1000 + 90 mu-m each of them, with          D051400100039 
           7.5 cm CsI scintillator detectors standing behind them D051400100040 
           are positioned outside the chamber.                    D051400100041
